Home Truein Help and Support Policies Can we setup a policy where staff record gets deleted after X days of absence? Can we setup a policy where staff record gets deleted after X days of absence? Yes, We do have a policy (P23) where we can set up auto deactivation of staff after x days of continuous absence. You can enable the policy from Settings > Policy > Add Policy. If policies are updated in middle of the month, will it update for previous days as well? Home Truein Help and Support Policies I need to mark overtime/extra-time based on staff’s working hours on daily/weekly basis. How can I do it? (Overtime policies) I need to mark overtime/extra-time based on staff’s working hours on daily/weekly basis. How can I do it? (Overtime policies) Admins can set policies to track overtime as per organization rules. It can be done as follows Setup up Overtime policy Admins need to enable the overtime approval policy from Settings > Policies > Click on Add new policy > Search “overtime” > list of all overtime-related policies will be displayed > Select and enable as required We have two ways to set it up – either apply a common rule or define it for each category of staff. There are certain pre-defined overtime policies like – Mark Overtime based on extra ‘Worked hours’ on a daily basis or weekly basis. – Add ‘Overtime’ only after a minimum of X minutes of extra work – Overtime rounding policy – Admin approval is required for all Overtime – Auto approve/reject Overtime requests after predefined days You can activate or deactivate them from the Settings > Policies section. Set up OT policies at the organization/site level or staff category level When the Overtime policy is enabled, choose if you want to enable it at the site level, staff category level, or shift level Enable approval policy If overtime requires approval then enable policy P49: Admin approval required for all Overtime Once this policy is enabled all overtime recorded will appear in ‘Alerts & Approvals’ section. Admins/Managers can approve/reject from here. Overtime view in Timesheet Overtime calculated based on the enabled policies on a daily or weekly basis will be visible in the Timesheet and daily Time Card of the staff. It will also be visible in Timesheet Report. Home Truein Help and Support Kiosk App What is PIN based attendance and how to set it up in Truein Kiosk devices? What is PIN based attendance and how to set it up in Truein Kiosk devices? In Truein alternative to the facial recognition feature, you can set PIN-based attendance for your staff. To set it up please refer to the below steps Step 1: Enable the “PIN Based Attendance” feature Go to Settings > Truein Features > Enable the “PIN Based Attendance” feature Step 2: Update the ‘Punch Mode’ on the Kiosk Devices Go to Settings > Kiosk Devices > Click on the three dots to edit the Kiosk Device > Scroll down to “Punch Mode” > Disable the “Face Recognition” functionality and enable the “PIN Authentication” functionality, if you want to capture a photo of your staff during PIN authentication you can enable the “Capture Photo with PIN” functionality. Please note this will capture the photo of the staff but no facial data will be used for authentication > Save Step 3: Assigning unique authentication PIN to employees Go to ‘Staff Directory’ > Search for the staff you want to assign PIN authentication > Edit > Click on “Enable PIN Based Attendance Authentication” under the ‘Access’ tab > You can assign a unique PIN to the staff or if left blank, the system will automatically assign a PIN to the staff > Save Once saved the system will send an email to the staff on their registered email id with the Attendance PIN, you can check the same from ‘System Logs’ as well You can check for the attendance PIN from the Staff Directory as well. Please ensure that the “Attendance PIN” column is enabled in the ‘Column Selector’ The Staff can now take the attendance from the Kiosk Device using their ‘Attendance PIN’ (Please ensure that the Kiosk Device is updated to the latest version) Click on Clock In > Enter the Attendance PIN > Click to Clock In > The Staff will be marked in Similarly for clocking out click on Clock Out > Enter the Attendance PIN > Click to Clock Out > The staff will be clocked out To edit the Attendance PIN manually please go to Staff Directory > Search for the staff you want to edit Attendance PIN > Edit > Update the Attendance PIN manually > Save, the updated PIN will be sent to the staff on their registered email id To re-generate the Attendance PIN by the system for the staff  please go to Staff Directory > Search for the staff you want to edit Attendance PIN > Click on the three dots in the ‘Action’ column > Click on ‘Regenarate PIN’ > The updated PIN will be sent to the staff on their registered email id Products Open menu Industry Open menu Solutions Open menu Pricing Customer Stories About Us Company Open menu Login Schedule a Demo Why Truein Face Attendance Testimonials Proudly powered by WordPress . Home Truein Help and Support Kiosk App Will Activity Punch be recorded in the offline mode? Will Activity Punch be recorded in the offline mode? Yes, you can mark Activity Punch in the offline mode from the Truein Kiosk device. In case the Kiosk device do not have a network connectivity your activity punches will still be recorded in the offline mode in the Kiosk Device. Once the device is online, the activity punches will be synced automatically. When you mark the Activity Punch in offline you will get a pop-up window stating that “Activity Punch recorded in offline mode” Once the Kiosk device is back online the Activity Punch will be synced. Home Truein Help and Support Kiosk App Can we setup a consent for staff before face registration from the Kiosk device? Can we setup a consent for staff before face registration from the Kiosk device? Yes, we can set up consent for the staff before face registration through the Kiosk device. Please refer to the below steps on how to set it up. Log in to the Admin web dashboard > Go to Settings > Kiosk Devices > Click on the ‘Kiosk Settings’ icon > Other Settings > Click on the check box “Face Recognition consent” to enable the same > Save Once this functionality is enabled, when an employee or staff register their faces for the first time from the Kiosk Device they will get a pop up consent for the same. Once the consent is accepted, the employee will be able to proceed with registering their face by clicking an onboarding photo. You can check the status of the “Face Consent” from the Staff Directory. If you want to reinitiate the consent, you can do that from Staff Directory > You will find the ‘reinitiate face registration consent’ icon by the accepted/rejected status under the ‘Face Consent’ column > Click on “Yes, Reinitiate Consent!” Products Open menu Industry Open menu Solutions Open menu Pricing Customer Stories About Us Company Open menu Login Schedule a Demo Why Truein Face Attendance Testimonials Proudly powered by WordPress . Home Truein Help and Support Kiosk App How to setup Kiosk App? How to setup Kiosk App? The kiosk app is set up on a standalone device like a tablet or supervisor’s phone. It works on any Android or iOS device. Please check device specs for the supported devices specifications: https://truein.com/website/marketing/device-specs.pdf Please follow the below steps to set up the kiosk app and register face via the Kiosk App. If you have not installed Kiosk App then follow Steps 1 to 3, else directly go to Step 4. Step 1 – Adding KIOSK Device on Dashboard. Get Activation key Go to Dashboard -> Settings -> Kiosk Devices -> Add KIOSK  -> Get Activation Key Step 2 – Download the App Play Store Link – https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.gotruein.kiosk App Store Link – https://apps.apple.com/in/app/truein-kiosk-not-for-staff/id1493367251 Step 3 – Enter Activation Key Step 4: Register Staff Face (For pending staff) If the staff’s baseline face is not registered, then they will appear in the Incomplete list. Complete the face registration of staff by clicking their name. You can search staff by their name, emp id, or date of birth. Click on three dots on top right corner > Go to Staff List > Select Staff (by name or emp id) and Take a clear picture Once the staff’s face is registered, they can do Clock In / Clock Out from the home screen. Other functions available in the Kiosk are as below. These functions can be enabled or disabled by admins from the web dashboard kiosk settings. – Staff List: You can Add new staff from the kiosk. enter their personal and work details, take a clear picture of their face, and complete add staff. You will see all staff uploaded via the web dashboard in the staff list. – Add a contractor agency from the kiosk. It will be enabled if the admin has granted access to this feature from the kiosk app. – Offline mode: If the internet is not available you can still continue taking attendance (clock in / out) via kiosk. All the photos will be stored in the kiosk and will be synced to the server when the internet is available. You can find the offline sync details in the offline sync section in a kiosk. – Raise Query to your HR/Admin: You can raise a query to your Manager/HR admin from Help and Support in the kiosk. The kiosk works in Touch and Touchless mode. You can also configure kiosks to do only Clock in or only Clock out. Go to Settings and Select Mode for the same. You can sync server configuration manually by clicking “Sync Kiosk” in the Settings section. Home Truein Help and Support Kiosk App Can we set separate kiosk devices for IN and OUT? Can we set separate kiosk devices for IN and OUT? Yes, you can do that. In the Kiosk App, in settings, you can select modes like Auto (both), Clock IN, and Clock OUT. The selected mode will be the one that will be set on that device. Home Truein Help and Support Kiosk App Can we restrict face re-registration (retake registration photo) on kiosk? Can we restrict face re-registration (retake registration photo) on kiosk? Yes, admins can disable access to retake registration photos from the kiosk. To disable access, log in to web dashboard and go to – Settings > Kiosk > Kiosk Settings > Action > Edit > Additional access on the kiosk Products Open menu Industry Open menu Solutions Open menu Pricing Customer Stories About Us Company Open menu Login Schedule a Demo Why Truein Face Attendance Testimonials Proudly powered by WordPress . Home Truein Help and Support Kiosk App If kiosk app is set default on device, screen will be on for whole day or it will go on sleep mode? If kiosk app is set default on device, screen will be on for whole day or it will go on sleep mode? No, if the kiosk app is set as the default app or if it’s open then it will not go into sleep mode until you manually lock the screen or turn on sleep mode. Home Truein Help and Support Kiosk App We dont want to add staff from kiosk app, can we disable this? We dont want to add staff from kiosk app, can we disable this? Yes, you can disable the Add staff from kiosk app option from Web dashboard > Settings > Kiosk > Kiosk settings > Edit kiosk > untick Add staff option > Save. Sync the kiosk app once, so it will not be visible on the kiosk device.
